+fn load_monster(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> Result<Option<Monster>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug, name, cr, armor_class, hit_points, tags FROM compendium_monsters WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(6, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 6 {
+        return Err("malformed monster row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Monster {

+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        cr: fields[2].to_string(),
+        armor_class: fields[3].parse().map_err(|_| "bad armor_class")?,
+        hit_points: fields[4].parse().map_err(|_| "bad hit_points")?,
+        tags: decode_string_list(fields[5]).ok_or_else(|| "bad tags".to_string())?,
+    }))

+
+fn load_item(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> Result<Option<Item>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug, name, item_type, rarity, cost_gp FROM compendium_items WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(5, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 5 {
+        return Err("malformed item row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Item {
+        slug: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        item_type: fields[2].to_string(),
+        rarity: fields[3].to_string(),
+        cost_gp: fields[4].parse().map_err(|_| "bad cost_gp")?,
+    }))
+}
+
+fn monster_create_json(monster: &Monster) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","cr":"{}","armor_class":{},"hit_points":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&monster.slug),
+        json_escape(&monster.name),
+        json_escape(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points
+    )
+}
+
+fn monster_read_json(monster: &Monster) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","cr":"{}","armor_class":{},"hit_points":{},"tags":[{}]}}"#,
+        json_escape(&monster.slug),
+        json_escape(&monster.name),
+        json_escape(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points,
+        string_array_json(&monster.tags)
+    )
+}
+
+fn item_json(item: &Item) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","type":"{}","rarity":"{}","cost_gp":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&item.slug),
+        json_escape(&item.name),
+        json_escape(&item.item_type),
+        json_escape(&item.rarity),
+        item.cost_gp
+    )
+}
+
+fn string_array_json(values: &[String]) -> String {
+    values
+        .iter()
+        .map(|value| format!(r#""{}""#, json_escape(value)))
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",")
+}
+
+fn encode_string_list(values: &[String]) -> String {
+    values
+        .iter()
+        .map(|value| hex_encode(value))
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",")
+}
+
+fn decode_string_list(encoded: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    if encoded.is_empty() {
+        return Some(Vec::new());
+    }
+    let mut values = Vec::new();
+    for value in encoded.split(',') {
+        values.push(hex_decode(value)?);
+    }
+    Some(values)
+}

+fn json_string_array_field(source: &str, key: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    let body = json_array_field(source, key)?;
+    parse_string_array_body(body)

 fn json_object_field<'a>(source: &'a str, key: &str) -> Option<&'a str> {
     let value = field_value(source, key)?;
     balanced_slice(value, '{', '}')
@@ -1121,6 +1464,56 @@
     objects

+fn parse_string_array_body(array_body: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    let mut values = Vec::new();
+    let mut rest = array_body.trim();
+    if rest.is_empty() {
+        return Some(values);
+    }
+    loop {
+        let (value, consumed) = parse_json_string_prefix(rest)?;
+        values.push(value);
+        rest = rest[consumed..].trim_start();
+        if rest.is_empty() {
+            return Some(values);
+        }
+        rest = rest.strip_prefix(',')?.trim_start();
+        if rest.is_empty() {
+            return None;
+        }
+    }
+}
+
+fn parse_json_string_prefix(source: &str) -> Option<(String, usize)> {
+    let bytes = source.as_bytes();
+    if bytes.first().copied()? != b'"' {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let mut out = String::new();
+    let mut escaped = false;
+    for (i, ch) in source[1..].char_indices() {
+        if escaped {
+            match ch {
+                '"' | '\\' | '/' => out.push(ch),
+                'n' => out.push('\n'),
+                'r' => out.push('\r'),
+                't' => out.push('\t'),
+                'b' => out.push('\u{0008}'),
+                'f' => out.push('\u{000c}'),
+                _ => return None,
+            }
+            escaped = false;
+        } else if ch == '\\' {
+            escaped = true;
+        } else if ch == '"' {
+            return Some((out, i + 2));
+        } else {
+            out.push(ch);
+        }
+    }
+    None
+}
+
 fn number_from_halves(value_twice: i64) -> String {
     if value_twice % 2 == 0 {
         (value_twice / 2).to_string()
@@ -1335,4 +1728,44 @@
             )
         );
     }
+

+    fn monster_json_matches_create_and_read_contract() {
+        let monster = parse_monster(
+            r#"{"slug":"goblin","name":"Goblin","cr":"1/4","armor_class":15,"hit_points":7,"tags":["humanoid","goblinoid"]}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+        assert_eq!(
+            monster_create_json(&monster),
+            r#"{"slug":"goblin","name":"Goblin","cr":"1/4","armor_class":15,"hit_points":7}"#
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            monster_read_json(&monster),
+            r#"{"slug":"goblin","name":"Goblin","cr":"1/4","armor_class":15,"hit_points":7,"tags":["humanoid","goblinoid"]}"#
+        );
+    }
+

+        let item = parse_item(
+            r#"{"slug":"healing-potion","name":"Potion of Healing","type":"potion","rarity":"common","cost_gp":50}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+        assert_eq!(
+            item_json(&item),
+            r#"{"slug":"healing-potion","name":"Potion of Healing","type":"potion","rarity":"common","cost_gp":50}"#
+        );
+    }
+

+    fn string_array_parser_accepts_empty_and_rejects_trailing_comma() {
+        assert_eq!(
+            json_string_array_field(r#"{"tags":[]}"#, "tags"),
+            Some(Vec::new())
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            json_string_array_field(r#"{"tags":["one",]}"#, "tags"),
+            None
+        );
+    }

+enum CompendiumResult {
+    Ok(String),
+    BadRequest,
+    NotFound,
+    Conflict,
+    StorageError,
+}
+
+fn create_monster(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    let monster = match parse_monster(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CompendiumResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if monster_exists(storage, &monster.slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO compendium_monsters (slug, name, cr, armor_class, hit_points, tags) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&monster.slug),
+        sql_string(&monster.name),
+        sql_string(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points,
+        sql_string(&encode_string_list(&monster.tags))
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CompendiumResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CompendiumResult::Ok(monster_create_json(&monster))
+}
+
+fn read_monster(slug: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    if !valid_slug(slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    match load_monster(storage, slug) {
+        Ok(Some(monster)) => CompendiumResult::Ok(monster_read_json(&monster)),
+        Ok(None) => CompendiumResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => CompendiumResult::StorageError,
+    }
+}
+
+fn create_item(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    let item = match parse_item(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CompendiumResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if item_exists(storage, &item.slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO compendium_items (slug, name, item_type, rarity, cost_gp) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&item.slug),
+        sql_string(&item.name),
+        sql_string(&item.item_type),
+        sql_string(&item.rarity),
+        item.cost_gp
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CompendiumResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CompendiumResult::Ok(item_json(&item))
+}
+
+fn read_item(slug: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    if !valid_slug(slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    match load_item(storage, slug) {
+        Ok(Some(item)) => CompendiumResult::Ok(item_json(&item)),
+        Ok(None) => CompendiumResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => CompendiumResult::StorageError,
+    }
+}
+
+fn parse_monster(body: &str) -> Option<Monster> {
+    let slug = json_string_field(body, "slug")?;
+    if !valid_slug(&slug) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let name = non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?;
+    let cr = non_empty_json_string(body, "cr")?;
+    let armor_class = json_i64_field(body, "armor_class")?;
+    let hit_points = json_i64_field(body, "hit_points")?;
+    let tags = json_string_array_field(body, "tags")?;
+    if armor_class < 0 || hit_points < 0 {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Monster {
+        slug,
+        name,
+        cr,
+        armor_class,
+        hit_points,
+        tags,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_item(body: &str) -> Option<Item> {
+    let slug = json_string_field(body, "slug")?;
+    if !valid_slug(&slug) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let name = non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?;
+    let item_type = non_empty_json_string(body, "type")?;
+    let rarity = non_empty_json_string(body, "rarity")?;
+    let cost_gp = json_i64_field(body, "cost_gp")?;
+    if cost_gp < 0 {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Item {
+        slug,
+        name,
+        item_type,
+        rarity,
+        cost_gp,
+    })
+}
+
+fn non_empty_json_string(body: &str, key: &str) -> Option<String> {
+    match json_string_field(body, key) {
+        Some(value) if !value.is_empty() => Some(value),
+        _ => None,
+    }
+}
+

+    !slug.is_empty()
+        && slug
+            .bytes()
+            .all(|b| b.is_ascii_lowercase() || b.is_ascii_digit() || b == b'-')

+fn parse_string_array_body(array_body: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    let mut values = Vec::new();
+    let mut rest = array_body.trim();
+    if rest.is_empty() {
+        return Some(values);
+    }
+    loop {
+        let (value, consumed) = parse_json_string_prefix(rest)?;
+        values.push(value);
+        rest = rest[consumed..].trim_start();
+        if rest.is_empty() {
+            return Some(values);
+        }
+        rest = rest.strip_prefix(',')?.trim_start();
+        if rest.is_empty() {
+            return None;
+        }
+    }
+}
+
+fn parse_json_string_prefix(source: &str) -> Option<(String, usize)> {
+    let bytes = source.as_bytes();
+    if bytes.first().copied()? != b'"' {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let mut out = String::new();
+    let mut escaped = false;
+    for (i, ch) in source[1..].char_indices() {
+        if escaped {
+            match ch {
+                '"' | '\\' | '/' => out.push(ch),
+                'n' => out.push('\n'),
+                'r' => out.push('\r'),
+                't' => out.push('\t'),
+                'b' => out.push('\u{0008}'),
+                'f' => out.push('\u{000c}'),
+                _ => return None,
+            }
+            escaped = false;
+        } else if ch == '\\' {
+            escaped = true;
+        } else if ch == '"' {
+            return Some((out, i + 2));
+        } else {
+            out.push(ch);
+        }
+    }
+    None
+}

+enum CompendiumResult {
+    Ok(String),
+    BadRequest,
+    NotFound,
+    Conflict,
+    StorageError,
+}
+
+fn create_monster(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    let monster = match parse_monster(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CompendiumResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if monster_exists(storage, &monster.slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO compendium_monsters (slug, name, cr, armor_class, hit_points, tags) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&monster.slug),
+        sql_string(&monster.name),
+        sql_string(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points,
+        sql_string(&encode_string_list(&monster.tags))
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CompendiumResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CompendiumResult::Ok(monster_create_json(&monster))
+}
+
+fn read_monster(slug: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    if !valid_slug(slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    match load_monster(storage, slug) {
+        Ok(Some(monster)) => CompendiumResult::Ok(monster_read_json(&monster)),
+        Ok(None) => CompendiumResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => CompendiumResult::StorageError,
+    }
+}
+
+fn create_item(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    let item = match parse_item(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CompendiumResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if item_exists(storage, &item.slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO compendium_items (slug, name, item_type, rarity, cost_gp) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&item.slug),
+        sql_string(&item.name),
+        sql_string(&item.item_type),
+        sql_string(&item.rarity),
+        item.cost_gp
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CompendiumResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CompendiumResult::Ok(item_json(&item))
+}
+
+fn read_item(slug: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    if !valid_slug(slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    match load_item(storage, slug) {
+        Ok(Some(item)) => CompendiumResult::Ok(item_json(&item)),
+        Ok(None) => CompendiumResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => CompendiumResult::StorageError,
+    }
+}
+
+fn parse_monster(body: &str) -> Option<Monster> {
+    let slug = json_string_field(body, "slug")?;
+    if !valid_slug(&slug) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let name = non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?;
+    let cr = non_empty_json_string(body, "cr")?;
+    let armor_class = json_i64_field(body, "armor_class")?;
+    let hit_points = json_i64_field(body, "hit_points")?;
+    let tags = json_string_array_field(body, "tags")?;
+    if armor_class < 0 || hit_points < 0 {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Monster {
+        slug,
+        name,
+        cr,
+        armor_class,
+        hit_points,
+        tags,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_item(body: &str) -> Option<Item> {
+    let slug = json_string_field(body, "slug")?;
+    if !valid_slug(&slug) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let name = non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?;
+    let item_type = non_empty_json_string(body, "type")?;
+    let rarity = non_empty_json_string(body, "rarity")?;
+    let cost_gp = json_i64_field(body, "cost_gp")?;
+    if cost_gp < 0 {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Item {
+        slug,
+        name,
+        item_type,
+        rarity,
+        cost_gp,
+    })
+}
+
+fn non_empty_json_string(body: &str, key: &str) -> Option<String> {
+    match json_string_field(body, key) {
+        Some(value) if !value.is_empty() => Some(value),
+        _ => None,
+    }
+}
+
+fn valid_slug(slug: &str) -> bool {
+    !slug.is_empty()
+        && slug
+            .bytes()
+            .all(|b| b.is_ascii_lowercase() || b.is_ascii_digit() || b == b'-')
+}
+
+fn monster_exists(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug FROM compendium_monsters WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn item_exists(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug FROM compendium_items WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn load_monster(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> Result<Option<Monster>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug, name, cr, armor_class, hit_points, tags FROM compendium_monsters WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(6, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 6 {
+        return Err("malformed monster row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Monster {
+        slug: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        cr: fields[2].to_string(),
+        armor_class: fields[3].parse().map_err(|_| "bad armor_class")?,
+        hit_points: fields[4].parse().map_err(|_| "bad hit_points")?,
+        tags: decode_string_list(fields[5]).ok_or_else(|| "bad tags".to_string())?,
+    }))
+}
+
+fn load_item(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> Result<Option<Item>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug, name, item_type, rarity, cost_gp FROM compendium_items WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(5, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 5 {
+        return Err("malformed item row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Item {
+        slug: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        item_type: fields[2].to_string(),
+        rarity: fields[3].to_string(),
+        cost_gp: fields[4].parse().map_err(|_| "bad cost_gp")?,
+    }))
+}
+
+fn monster_create_json(monster: &Monster) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","cr":"{}","armor_class":{},"hit_points":{}}}"#,

+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points

+
+fn monster_read_json(monster: &Monster) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","cr":"{}","armor_class":{},"hit_points":{},"tags":[{}]}}"#,
+        json_escape(&monster.slug),
+        json_escape(&monster.name),
+        json_escape(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,

+fn item_json(item: &Item) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","type":"{}","rarity":"{}","cost_gp":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&item.slug),
+        json_escape(&item.name),
+        json_escape(&item.item_type),
+        json_escape(&item.rarity),
+        item.cost_gp

+fn string_array_json(values: &[String]) -> String {
+    values
+        .iter()
+        .map(|value| format!(r#""{}""#, json_escape(value)))
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",")

+fn encode_string_list(values: &[String]) -> String {
+    values
+        .iter()
+        .map(|value| hex_encode(value))
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",")

+fn parse_string_array_body(array_body: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    let mut values = Vec::new();
+    let mut rest = array_body.trim();
+    if rest.is_empty() {
+        return Some(values);
+    }
+    loop {
+        let (value, consumed) = parse_json_string_prefix(rest)?;
+        values.push(value);
+        rest = rest[consumed..].trim_start();
+        if rest.is_empty() {
+            return Some(values);
+        }
+        rest = rest.strip_prefix(',')?.trim_start();
+        if rest.is_empty() {
+            return None;
+        }
+    }
+}
+
+fn parse_json_string_prefix(source: &str) -> Option<(String, usize)> {
+    let bytes = source.as_bytes();
+    if bytes.first().copied()? != b'"' {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let mut out = String::new();
+    let mut escaped = false;
+    for (i, ch) in source[1..].char_indices() {
+        if escaped {
+            match ch {
+                '"' | '\\' | '/' => out.push(ch),
+                'n' => out.push('\n'),
+                'r' => out.push('\r'),
+                't' => out.push('\t'),
+                'b' => out.push('\u{0008}'),
+                'f' => out.push('\u{000c}'),
+                _ => return None,
+            }
+            escaped = false;
+        } else if ch == '\\' {
+            escaped = true;
+        } else if ch == '"' {
+            return Some((out, i + 2));
+        } else {
+            out.push(ch);
+        }
+    }
+    None
+}
+
 fn number_from_halves(value_twice: i64) -> String {
     if value_twice % 2 == 0 {
         (value_twice / 2).to_string()
@@ -1335,4 +1728,44 @@
             )
         );
     }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn monster_json_matches_create_and_read_contract() {
+        let monster = parse_monster(
+            r#"{"slug":"goblin","name":"Goblin","cr":"1/4","armor_class":15,"hit_points":7,"tags":["humanoid","goblinoid"]}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+        assert_eq!(
+            monster_create_json(&monster),
+            r#"{"slug":"goblin","name":"Goblin","cr":"1/4","armor_class":15,"hit_points":7}"#
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            monster_read_json(&monster),
+            r#"{"slug":"goblin","name":"Goblin","cr":"1/4","armor_class":15,"hit_points":7,"tags":["humanoid","goblinoid"]}"#
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn item_json_matches_contract() {
+        let item = parse_item(
+            r#"{"slug":"healing-potion","name":"Potion of Healing","type":"potion","rarity":"common","cost_gp":50}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+        assert_eq!(
+            item_json(&item),
+            r#"{"slug":"healing-potion","name":"Potion of Healing","type":"potion","rarity":"common","cost_gp":50}"#
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn string_array_parser_accepts_empty_and_rejects_trailing_comma() {
+        assert_eq!(
+            json_string_array_field(r#"{"tags":[]}"#, "tags"),
+            Some(Vec::new())
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            json_string_array_field(r#"{"tags":["one",]}"#, "tags"),
+            None
+        );
+    }

+enum CompendiumResult {
+    Ok(String),
+    BadRequest,
+    NotFound,
+    Conflict,
+    StorageError,
+}
+
+fn create_monster(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    let monster = match parse_monster(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CompendiumResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if monster_exists(storage, &monster.slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO compendium_monsters (slug, name, cr, armor_class, hit_points, tags) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&monster.slug),
+        sql_string(&monster.name),
+        sql_string(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points,
+        sql_string(&encode_string_list(&monster.tags))
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CompendiumResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CompendiumResult::Ok(monster_create_json(&monster))
+}
+
+fn read_monster(slug: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    if !valid_slug(slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    match load_monster(storage, slug) {
+        Ok(Some(monster)) => CompendiumResult::Ok(monster_read_json(&monster)),
+        Ok(None) => CompendiumResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => CompendiumResult::StorageError,
+    }
+}
+
+fn create_item(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    let item = match parse_item(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CompendiumResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if item_exists(storage, &item.slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO compendium_items (slug, name, item_type, rarity, cost_gp) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&item.slug),
+        sql_string(&item.name),
+        sql_string(&item.item_type),
+        sql_string(&item.rarity),
+        item.cost_gp
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CompendiumResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CompendiumResult::Ok(item_json(&item))
+}
+
+fn read_item(slug: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    if !valid_slug(slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    match load_item(storage, slug) {
+        Ok(Some(item)) => CompendiumResult::Ok(item_json(&item)),
+        Ok(None) => CompendiumResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => CompendiumResult::StorageError,
+    }
+}
+
+fn parse_monster(body: &str) -> Option<Monster> {
+    let slug = json_string_field(body, "slug")?;
+    if !valid_slug(&slug) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let name = non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?;
+    let cr = non_empty_json_string(body, "cr")?;
+    let armor_class = json_i64_field(body, "armor_class")?;
+    let hit_points = json_i64_field(body, "hit_points")?;
+    let tags = json_string_array_field(body, "tags")?;
+    if armor_class < 0 || hit_points < 0 {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Monster {
+        slug,
+        name,
+        cr,
+        armor_class,
+        hit_points,
+        tags,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_item(body: &str) -> Option<Item> {
+    let slug = json_string_field(body, "slug")?;
+    if !valid_slug(&slug) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let name = non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?;
+    let item_type = non_empty_json_string(body, "type")?;
+    let rarity = non_empty_json_string(body, "rarity")?;
+    let cost_gp = json_i64_field(body, "cost_gp")?;
+    if cost_gp < 0 {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Item {
+        slug,
+        name,
+        item_type,
+        rarity,
+        cost_gp,
+    })
+}
+
+fn non_empty_json_string(body: &str, key: &str) -> Option<String> {
+    match json_string_field(body, key) {
+        Some(value) if !value.is_empty() => Some(value),
+        _ => None,
+    }
+}
+
+fn valid_slug(slug: &str) -> bool {
+    !slug.is_empty()
+        && slug
+            .bytes()
+            .all(|b| b.is_ascii_lowercase() || b.is_ascii_digit() || b == b'-')
+}
+
+fn monster_exists(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug FROM compendium_monsters WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn item_exists(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug FROM compendium_items WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn load_monster(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> Result<Option<Monster>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug, name, cr, armor_class, hit_points, tags FROM compendium_monsters WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(6, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 6 {
+        return Err("malformed monster row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Monster {
+        slug: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        cr: fields[2].to_string(),
+        armor_class: fields[3].parse().map_err(|_| "bad armor_class")?,
+        hit_points: fields[4].parse().map_err(|_| "bad hit_points")?,
+        tags: decode_string_list(fields[5]).ok_or_else(|| "bad tags".to_string())?,
+    }))
+}
+
+fn load_item(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> Result<Option<Item>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug, name, item_type, rarity, cost_gp FROM compendium_items WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(5, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 5 {
+        return Err("malformed item row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Item {
+        slug: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        item_type: fields[2].to_string(),
+        rarity: fields[3].to_string(),
+        cost_gp: fields[4].parse().map_err(|_| "bad cost_gp")?,
+    }))
+}
+
+fn monster_create_json(monster: &Monster) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","cr":"{}","armor_class":{},"hit_points":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&monster.slug),
+        json_escape(&monster.name),
+        json_escape(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points
+    )
+}
+
+fn monster_read_json(monster: &Monster) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","cr":"{}","armor_class":{},"hit_points":{},"tags":[{}]}}"#,
+        json_escape(&monster.slug),
+        json_escape(&monster.name),
+        json_escape(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points,
+        string_array_json(&monster.tags)
+    )
+}
+
+fn item_json(item: &Item) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","type":"{}","rarity":"{}","cost_gp":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&item.slug),
+        json_escape(&item.name),
+        json_escape(&item.item_type),
+        json_escape(&item.rarity),
+        item.cost_gp
+    )
+}
+
+fn string_array_json(values: &[String]) -> String {
+    values
+        .iter()
+        .map(|value| format!(r#""{}""#, json_escape(value)))
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",")
+}
+
+fn encode_string_list(values: &[String]) -> String {
+    values
+        .iter()
+        .map(|value| hex_encode(value))
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",")
+}
+
+fn decode_string_list(encoded: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    if encoded.is_empty() {
+        return Some(Vec::new());
+    }
+    let mut values = Vec::new();
+    for value in encoded.split(',') {
+        values.push(hex_decode(value)?);
+    }
+    Some(values)
+}

+fn json_string_array_field(source: &str, key: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    let body = json_array_field(source, key)?;
+    parse_string_array_body(body)
+}

 fn json_object_field<'a>(source: &'a str, key: &str) -> Option<&'a str> {
     let value = field_value(source, key)?;
     balanced_slice(value, '{', '}')
@@ -1121,6 +1464,56 @@

+fn parse_string_array_body(array_body: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    let mut values = Vec::new();
+    let mut rest = array_body.trim();
+    if rest.is_empty() {
+        return Some(values);
+    }
+    loop {
+        let (value, consumed) = parse_json_string_prefix(rest)?;
+        values.push(value);
+        rest = rest[consumed..].trim_start();
+        if rest.is_empty() {
+            return Some(values);
+        }
+        rest = rest.strip_prefix(',')?.trim_start();
+        if rest.is_empty() {
+            return None;
+        }
+    }
+}
+
+fn parse_json_string_prefix(source: &str) -> Option<(String, usize)> {
+    let bytes = source.as_bytes();
+    if bytes.first().copied()? != b'"' {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let mut out = String::new();
+    let mut escaped = false;
+    for (i, ch) in source[1..].char_indices() {
+        if escaped {
+            match ch {
+                '"' | '\\' | '/' => out.push(ch),
+                'n' => out.push('\n'),
+                'r' => out.push('\r'),
+                't' => out.push('\t'),
+                'b' => out.push('\u{0008}'),
+                'f' => out.push('\u{000c}'),
+                _ => return None,
+            }
+            escaped = false;
+        } else if ch == '\\' {
+            escaped = true;
+        } else if ch == '"' {
+            return Some((out, i + 2));
+        } else {
+            out.push(ch);
+        }
+    }
+    None
+}
+

     if value_twice % 2 == 0 {
         (value_twice / 2).to_string()

         );
     }

  1172	    if session.order.is_empty() {
  1173	        return CombatResult::BadRequest;
  1174	    }
  1175	
  1176	    session.turn_index += 1;
  1177	    if session.turn_index >= session.order.len() {
  1178	        session.turn_index = 0;
  1179	        session.round += 1;
  1180	    }
  1181	
  1182	    let active = &mut session.order[session.turn_index];
  1183	    for condition in &mut active.conditions {
  1184	        condition.remaining_rounds -= 1;
  1185	    }
  1186	    active
  1187	        .conditions
  1188	        .retain(|condition| condition.remaining_rounds > 0);
  1189	
  1190	    CombatResult::Ok(combat_session_advanced_json(session))
  1191	}
  1192	
  1193	fn combat_session_created_json(session: &CombatSession) -> String {
  1194	    let active = &session.order[session.turn_index];
  1195	    format!(
  1196	        r#"{{"id":"{}","round":{},"turn_index":{},"active":{},"order":[{}]}}"#,
  1197	        json_escape(&session.id),
  1198	        session.round,
  1199	        session.turn_index,
  1200	        active_combatant_json(active),
  1201	        initiative_entries_json(&session.order)
  1202	    )
  1203	}

  1247	fn session_conditions_json(session: &CombatSession) -> String {
  1248	    let entries: Vec<String> = session
  1249	        .order
  1250	        .iter()
  1251	        .filter(|combatant| combatant.had_conditions || !combatant.conditions.is_empty())
  1252	        .map(|combatant| {

  1258	        })
  1259	        .collect();

  1263	fn character_ability_modifier(body: &str) -> Option<String> {

  1265	    validate_ability_score(score)?;

  1270	fn character_proficiency(body: &str) -> Option<String> {

  1272	    let proficiency_bonus = proficiency_bonus(level)?;
  1273	    Some(format!(

  1278	fn character_derived_stats(body: &str) -> Option<String> {
  1279	    let level = json_i64_field(body, "level")?;
  1280	    let proficiency_bonus = proficiency_bonus(level)?;
  1281	    let abilities = json_object_field(body, "abilities")?;
  1282	    let armor = json_object_field(body, "armor")?;
  1283	
  1284	    let str_mod = ability_modifier_from_field(abilities, "str")?;
  1285	    let dex_mod = ability_modifier_from_field(abilities, "dex")?;
  1286	    let con_mod = ability_modifier_from_field(abilities, "con")?;
  1287	    let int_mod = ability_modifier_from_field(abilities, "int")?;
  1288	    let wis_mod = ability_modifier_from_field(abilities, "wis")?;
  1289	    let cha_mod = ability_modifier_from_field(abilities, "cha")?;
  1290	
  1291	    let armor_base = json_i64_field(armor, "base")?;
  1292	    let shield = json_bool_field(armor, "shield")?;
  1293	    let dex_cap = json_i64_field(armor, "dex_cap")?;
  1294	    let shield_bonus = if shield { 2 } else { 0 };
  1295	    let hp_max = level * (6 + con_mod);
  1296	    let armor_class = armor_base + dex_mod.min(dex_cap) + shield_bonus;
  1297	
  1298	    Some(format!(
  1299	        r#"{{"level":{level},"proficiency_bonus":{proficiency_bonus},"hp_max":{hp_max},"armor_class":{armor_class},"modifiers":{{"str":{str_mod},"dex":{dex_mod},"con":{con_mod},"int":{int_mod},"wis":{wis_mod},"cha":{cha_mod}}}}}"#
  1300	    ))
  1301	}
  1302	
  1303	fn ability_modifier_from_field(source: &str, key: &str) -> Option<i64> {
  1304	    let score = json_i64_field(source, key)?;
  1305	    validate_ability_score(score)?;
  1306	    Some(ability_modifier(score))
  1307	}
  1308	
  1309	fn validate_ability_score(score: i64) -> Option<()> {
  1310	    if (1..=30).contains(&score) {
  1311	        Some(())
  1312	    } else {
  1313	        None
  1314	    }
  1315	}
  1316	
  1317	fn ability_modifier(score: i64) -> i64 {
  1318	    (score - 10).div_euclid(2)
  1319	}
  1320	
  1321	fn proficiency_bonus(level: i64) -> Option<i64> {
  1322	    match level {
  1323	        1..=4 => Some(2),
  1324	        5..=8 => Some(3),
  1325	        9..=12 => Some(4),
  1326	        13..=16 => Some(5),
  1327	        17..=20 => Some(6),
  1328	        _ => None,
  1329	    }
  1330	}
  1331	
  1332	fn json_string_field(source: &str, key: &str) -> Option<String> {
  1333	    let value = field_value(source, key)?;
  1334	    let bytes = value.as_bytes();
  1335	    if bytes.first().copied()? != b'"' {
  1336	        return None;
  1337	    }
  1338	    let mut out = String::new();
  1339	    let mut escaped = false;
  1340	    for (i, ch) in value[1..].char_indices() {
  1341	        if escaped {
  1342	            match ch {
  1343	                '"' | '\\' | '/' => out.push(ch),
  1344	                'n' => out.push('\n'),
  1345	                'r' => out.push('\r'),
  1346	                't' => out.push('\t'),
  1347	                'b' => out.push('\u{0008}'),
  1348	                'f' => out.push('\u{000c}'),
  1349	                _ => return None,
  1350	            }
  1351	            escaped = false;
  1352	        } else if ch == '\\' {
  1353	            escaped = true;
  1354	        } else if ch == '"' {
  1355	            return Some(out);
  1356	        } else {
  1357	            out.push(ch);
  1358	        }
  1359	        let _ = i;
  1360	    }
  1361	    None
  1362	}
  1363	
  1364	fn json_i64_field(source: &str, key: &str) -> Option<i64> {
  1365	    let value = field_value(source, key)?;
  1366	    let mut end = 0;
  1367	    for (i, ch) in value.char_indices() {
  1368	        if i == 0 && ch == '-' {
  1369	            end = 1;
  1370	        } else if ch.is_ascii_digit() {
  1371	            end = i + ch.len_utf8();
  1372	        } else {
  1373	            break;
  1374	        }
  1375	    }
  1376	    if end == 0 || &value[..end] == "-" {
  1377	        return None;
  1378	    }
  1379	    value[..end].parse().ok()
  1380	}
  1381	
  1382	fn json_array_field<'a>(source: &'a str, key: &str) -> Option<&'a str> {
  1383	    let value = field_value(source, key)?;
  1384	    balanced_slice(value, '[', ']')
  1385	}
  1386	
  1387	fn json_string_array_field(source: &str, key: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
  1388	    let body = json_array_field(source, key)?;
  1389	    parse_string_array_body(body)
  1390	}
  1391	
  1392	fn json_object_field<'a>(source: &'a str, key: &str) -> Option<&'a str> {
  1393	    let value = field_value(source, key)?;
  1394	    balanced_slice(value, '{', '}')
  1395	}
  1396	
  1397	fn json_bool_field(source: &str, key: &str) -> Option<bool> {
  1398	    let value = field_value(source, key)?;
  1399	    if value.starts_with("true") {
  1400	        Some(true)
  1401	    } else if value.starts_with("false") {
  1402	        Some(false)
  1403	    } else {
  1404	        None
  1405	    }
  1406	}
  1407	
  1408	fn field_value<'a>(source: &'a str, key: &str) -> Option<&'a str> {
  1409	    let needle = format!(r#""{key}""#);
  1410	    let start = source.find(&needle)? + needle.len();
  1411	    let after_key = source[start..].trim_start();
  1412	    let after_colon = after_key.strip_prefix(':')?.trim_start();
  1413	    Some(after_colon)
  1414	}
  1415	
  1416	fn balanced_slice(source: &str, open: char, close: char) -> Option<&str> {
  1417	    if !source.starts_with(open) {
  1418	        return None;
  1419	    }
  1420	    let mut depth = 0_i32;
  1421	    let mut in_string = false;
  1422	    let mut escaped = false;
  1423	    for (i, ch) in source.char_indices() {
  1424	        if in_string {
  1425	            if escaped {
  1426	                escaped = false;
  1427	            } else if ch == '\\' {
  1428	                escaped = true;
  1429	            } else if ch == '"' {
  1430	                in_string = false;
  1431	            }
  1432	            continue;
  1433	        }
  1434	        if ch == '"' {
  1435	            in_string = true;
  1436	        } else if ch == open {
  1437	            depth += 1;
  1438	        } else if ch == close {
  1439	            depth -= 1;
  1440	            if depth == 0 {
  1441	                return Some(&source[1..i]);
  1442	            }
  1443	        }
  1444	    }
  1445	    None
  1446	}
  1447	
  1448	fn array_objects(array_body: &str) -> Vec<&str> {
  1449	    let mut objects = Vec::new();
  1450	    let mut rest = array_body.trim();
  1451	    while !rest.is_empty() {
  1452	        if let Some(start) = rest.find('{') {
  1453	            rest = &rest[start..];
  1454	            if let Some(object) = balanced_slice(rest, '{', '}') {
  1455	                objects.push(object);
  1456	                let consumed = object.len() + 2;
  1457	                rest = rest[consumed..].trim_start();
  1458	                if let Some(next) = rest.strip_prefix(',') {
  1459	                    rest = next.trim_start();
  1460	                }
  1461	            } else {
  1462	                break;
  1463	            }
  1464	        } else {
  1465	            break;
  1466	        }
  1467	    }
  1468	    objects
  1469	}
  1470	
  1471	fn parse_string_array_body(array_body: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
  1472	    let mut values = Vec::new();
  1473	    let mut rest = array_body.trim();
  1474	    if rest.is_empty() {
  1475	        return Some(values);
  1476	    }
  1477	    loop {
  1478	        let (value, consumed) = parse_json_string_prefix(rest)?;
  1479	        values.push(value);
  1480	        rest = rest[consumed..].trim_start();
  1481	        if rest.is_empty() {
  1482	            return Some(values);
  1483	        }
  1484	        rest = rest.strip_prefix(',')?.trim_start();
  1485	        if rest.is_empty() {
  1486	            return None;
  1487	        }
  1488	    }
  1489	}
  1490	
  1491	fn parse_json_string_prefix(source: &str) -> Option<(String, usize)> {
  1492	    let bytes = source.as_bytes();
  1493	    if bytes.first().copied()? != b'"' {
  1494	        return None;
  1495	    }
  1496	    let mut out = String::new();
  1497	    let mut escaped = false;
  1498	    for (i, ch) in source[1..].char_indices() {
  1499	        if escaped {
  1500	            match ch {
  1501	                '"' | '\\' | '/' => out.push(ch),
  1502	                'n' => out.push('\n'),
  1503	                'r' => out.push('\r'),
  1504	                't' => out.push('\t'),
  1505	                'b' => out.push('\u{0008}'),
  1506	                'f' => out.push('\u{000c}'),
  1507	                _ => return None,
  1508	            }
  1509	            escaped = false;
  1510	        } else if ch == '\\' {
  1511	            escaped = true;
  1512	        } else if ch == '"' {
  1513	            return Some((out, i + 2));
  1514	        } else {
  1515	            out.push(ch);
  1516	        }
  1517	    }
  1518	    None
  1519	}

    69	fn main() -> std::io::Result<()> {
    70	    let port = env::var("PORT").unwrap_or_else(|_| "8080".to_string());
    71	    let storage = Arc::new(Mutex::new(Storage {
    72	        db_path: DB_PATH.to_string(),
    73	    }));
    74	    if let Err(err) = init_storage(&storage.lock().unwrap()) {
    75	        eprintln!("storage initialization failed: {err}");
    76	    }
    77	    let sessions = Arc::new(Mutex::new(load_combat_sessions(&storage.lock().unwrap())));
    78	    let users = Arc::new(Mutex::new(load_users(&storage.lock().unwrap())));
    79	    let listener = TcpListener::bind(format!("127.0.0.1:{port}"))?;
    80	    for stream in listener.incoming() {
    81	        if let Ok(mut stream) = stream {
    82	            let _ = handle(&mut stream, &sessions, &users, &storage);
    83	        }
    84	    }
    85	    Ok(())
    86	}

    88	fn handle(
    89	    stream: &mut TcpStream,
    90	    sessions: &Sessions,
    91	    users: &Users,
    92	    storage: &StorageState,
    93	) -> std::io::Result<()> {
    94	    let req = read_request(stream)?;
    95	    let (head, body) = split_request(&req);
    96	    let first = head.lines().next().unwrap_or("");
    97	    let mut parts = first.split_whitespace();
    98	    let method = parts.next().unwrap_or("");
    99	    let path = parts.next().unwrap_or("");
   100

   102	        ("GET", "/health") => respond(stream, 200, r#"{"ok":true}"#),
   103	        ("GET", "/v1/storage/status") => {

   105	            respond(

   111	            )

   117	                users.lock().unwrap().clear();

   119	                    stream,
   120	                    200,
   121	                    &format!(r#"{{"ok":true,"schema_version":{SCHEMA_VERSION}}}"#),
   122	                )

   199	                CompendiumResult::Conflict => respond(stream, 409, r#"{"error":"conflict"}"#),
   200	                CompendiumResult::StorageError => {
   201	                    respond(stream, 500, r#"{"error":"storage error"}"#)
   202	                }
   203	            }
   204	        }
   205	        ("POST", "/v1/compendium/items") => match create_item(body, &storage.lock().unwrap()) {
   206	            CompendiumResult::Ok(json) => respond(stream, 201, &json),
   207	            CompendiumResult::BadRequest => respond(stream, 400, r#"{"error":"bad request"}"#),
   208	            CompendiumResult::NotFound => respond(stream, 404, r#"{"error":"not found"}"#),
   209	            CompendiumResult::Conflict => respond(stream, 409, r#"{"error":"conflict"}"#),
   210	            CompendiumResult::StorageError => respond(stream, 500, r#"{"error":"storage error"}"#),
   211	        },

   681	fn cr_xp(cr: &str) -> Option<i64> {
   682	    match cr {
   683	        "0" => Some(10),
   684	        "1/8" => Some(25),
   685	        "1/4" => Some(50),
   686	        "1/2" => Some(100),
   687	        "1" => Some(200),
   688	        "2" => Some(450),
   689	        "3" => Some(700),
   690	        "4" => Some(1100),
   691	        "5" => Some(1800),
   692	        _ => None,
   693	    }
   694	}

   696	fn monster_multiplier_twice(count: i64) -> i64 {
   697	    match count {
   698	        1 => 2,
   699	        2 => 3,
   700	        3..=6 => 4,
   701	        7..=10 => 5,
   702	        11..=14 => 6,
   703	        15.. => 8,
   704	        _ => 2,
   705	    }
   706	}

   708	fn initiative_order(body: &str) -> Option<String> {
   709	    let combatants = json_array_field(body, "combatants")?;
   710	    let mut rows = Vec::new();
   711	    for combatant in array_objects(combatants) {
   712	        let name = json_string_field(combatant, "name")?;
   713	        let dex = json_i64_field(combatant, "dex")?;
   714	        let roll = json_i64_field(combatant, "roll")?;
   715	        rows.push((name, dex, roll + dex));
   716	    }
   717	    rows.sort_by(|a, b| {
   718	        b.2.cmp(&a.2)
   719	            .then_with(|| b.1.cmp(&a.1))
   720	            .then_with(|| a.0.cmp(&b.0))
   721	    });
   722	
   723	    let entries: Vec<String> = rows
   724	        .into_iter()
   725	        .map(|(name, _, score)| format!(r#"{{"name":"{}","score":{score}}}"#, json_escape(&name)))
   726	        .collect();
   727	    Some(format!(r#"{{"order":[{}]}}"#, entries.join(",")))
   728	}

   751	fn create_monster(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
   752	    let monster = match parse_monster(body) {
   753	        Some(value) => value,
   754	        None => return CompendiumResult::BadRequest,
   755	    };
   756	    if monster_exists(storage, &monster.slug) {
   757	        return CompendiumResult::Conflict;
   758	    }
   759	    let sql = format!(
   760	        "INSERT INTO compendium_monsters (slug, name, cr, armor_class, hit_points, tags) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
   761	        sql_string(&monster.slug),
   762	        sql_string(&monster.name),
   763	        sql_string(&monster.cr),
   764	        monster.armor_class,
   765	        monster.hit_points,
   766	        sql_string(&encode_string_list(&monster.tags))
   767	    );
   768	    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
   769	        return CompendiumResult::StorageError;
   770	    }
   771	    CompendiumResult::Ok(monster_create_json(&monster))
   772	}
   773	
   774	fn read_monster(slug: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
   775	    if !valid_slug(slug) {
   776	        return CompendiumResult::BadRequest;
   777	    }
   778	    match load_monster(storage, slug) {
   779	        Ok(Some(monster)) => CompendiumResult::Ok(monster_read_json(&monster)),
   780	        Ok(None) => CompendiumResult::NotFound,
   781	        Err(_) => CompendiumResult::StorageError,
   782	    }
   783	}
   784	
   785	fn create_item(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
   786	    let item = match parse_item(body) {
   787	        Some(value) => value,
   788	        None => return CompendiumResult::BadRequest,
   789	    };
   790	    if item_exists(storage, &item.slug) {
   791	        return CompendiumResult::Conflict;
   792	    }
   793	    let sql = format!(
   794	        "INSERT INTO compendium_items (slug, name, item_type, rarity, cost_gp) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
   795	        sql_string(&item.slug),
   796	        sql_string(&item.name),
   797	        sql_string(&item.item_type),
   798	        sql_string(&item.rarity),
   799	        item.cost_gp
   800	    );
   801	    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
   802	        return CompendiumResult::StorageError;
   803	    }
   804	    CompendiumResult::Ok(item_json(&item))
   805	}
   806	
   807	fn read_item(slug: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
   808	    if !valid_slug(slug) {
   809	        return CompendiumResult::BadRequest;
   810	    }
   811	    match load_item(storage, slug) {
   812	        Ok(Some(item)) => CompendiumResult::Ok(item_json(&item)),
   813	        Ok(None) => CompendiumResult::NotFound,
   814	        Err(_) => CompendiumResult::StorageError,
   815	    }
   816	}
   817	
   818	fn parse_monster(body: &str) -> Option<Monster> {
   819	    let slug = json_string_field(body, "slug")?;
   820	    if !valid_slug(&slug) {
   821	        return None;
   822	    }
   823	    let name = non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?;
   824	    let cr = non_empty_json_string(body, "cr")?;
   825	    let armor_class = json_i64_field(body, "armor_class")?;
   826	    let hit_points = json_i64_field(body, "hit_points")?;
   827	    let tags = json_string_array_field(body, "tags")?;
   828	    if armor_class < 0 || hit_points < 0 {
   829	        return None;
   830	    }
   831	    Some(Monster {
   832	        slug,
   833	        name,
   834	        cr,
   835	        armor_class,
   836	        hit_points,
   837	        tags,
   838	    })
   839	}
   840	
   841	fn parse_item(body: &str) -> Option<Item> {
   842	    let slug = json_string_field(body, "slug")?;
   843	    if !valid_slug(&slug) {
   844	        return None;
   845	    }
   846	    let name = non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?;
   847	    let item_type = non_empty_json_string(body, "type")?;
   848	    let rarity = non_empty_json_string(body, "rarity")?;
   849	    let cost_gp = json_i64_field(body, "cost_gp")?;
   850	    if cost_gp < 0 {
   851	        return None;
   852	    }
   853	    Some(Item {
   854	        slug,
   855	        name,
   856	        item_type,
   857	        rarity,
   858	        cost_gp,
   859	    })
   860	}
   861	
   862	fn non_empty_json_string(body: &str, key: &str) -> Option<String> {
   863	    match json_string_field(body, key) {
   864	        Some(value) if !value.is_empty() => Some(value),
   865	        _ => None,
   866	    }
   867	}
   868	
   869	fn valid_slug(slug: &str) -> bool {
   870	    !slug.is_empty()
   871	        && slug
   872	            .bytes()
   873	            .all(|b| b.is_ascii_lowercase() || b.is_ascii_digit() || b == b'-')
   874	}
   875	
   876	fn monster_exists(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> bool {
   877	    query_sql(
   878	        storage,
   879	        &format!(
   880	            "SELECT slug FROM compendium_monsters WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
   881	            sql_string(slug)
   882	        ),
   883	    )
   884	    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
   885	    .unwrap_or(false)
   886	}
   887	
   888	fn item_exists(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> bool {
   889	    query_sql(
   890	        storage,
   891	        &format!(
   892	            "SELECT slug FROM compendium_items WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
   893	            sql_string(slug)
   894	        ),
   895	    )
   896	    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
   897	    .unwrap_or(false)
   898	}
   899	
   900	fn load_monster(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> Result<Option<Monster>, String> {
   901	    let out = query_sql(
   902	        storage,
   903	        &format!(
   904	            "SELECT slug, name, cr, armor_class, hit_points, tags FROM compendium_monsters WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
   905	            sql_string(slug)
   906	        ),
   907	    )?;
   908	    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
   909	        return Ok(None);
   910	    };
   911	    let fields = line.splitn(6, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
   912	    if fields.len() != 6 {
   913	        return Err("malformed monster row".to_string());
   914	    }
   915	    Ok(Some(Monster {
   916	        slug: fields[0].to_string(),
   917	        name: fields[1].to_string(),
   918	        cr: fields[2].to_string(),
   919	        armor_class: fields[3].parse().map_err(|_| "bad armor_class")?,
   920	        hit_points: fields[4].parse().map_err(|_| "bad hit_points")?,
   921	        tags: decode_string_list(fields[5]).ok_or_else(|| "bad tags".to_string())?,
   922	    }))
   923	}
   924	
   925	fn load_item(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> Result<Option<Item>, String> {
   926	    let out = query_sql(
   927	        storage,
   928	        &format!(
   929	            "SELECT slug, name, item_type, rarity, cost_gp FROM compendium_items WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
   930	            sql_string(slug)
   931	        ),
   932	    )?;
   933	    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
   934	        return Ok(None);
   935	    };
   936	    let fields = line.splitn(5, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
   937	    if fields.len() != 5 {
   938	        return Err("malformed item row".to_string());
   939	    }
   940	    Ok(Some(Item {
   941	        slug: fields[0].to_string(),
   942	        name: fields[1].to_string(),
   943	        item_type: fields[2].to_string(),
   944	        rarity: fields[3].to_string(),
   945	        cost_gp: fields[4].parse().map_err(|_| "bad cost_gp")?,
   946	    }))
   947	}

   982	
   983	fn string_array_json(values: &[String]) -> String {
   984	    values
   985	        .iter()
   986	        .map(|value| format!(r#""{}""#, json_escape(value)))
   987	        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
   988	        .join(",")
   989	}
   990	
   991	fn encode_string_list(values: &[String]) -> String {
   992	    values
   993	        .iter()
   994	        .map(|value| hex_encode(value))
   995	        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
   996	        .join(",")
   997	}
   998	
   999	fn decode_string_list(encoded: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
  1000	    if encoded.is_empty() {
  1001	        return Some(Vec::new());
  1002	    }
  1003	    let mut values = Vec::new();
  1004	    for value in encoded.split(',') {
  1005	        values.push(hex_decode(value)?);
  1006	    }
  1007	    Some(values)
  1008	}

  1010	fn register_user(body: &str, users: &mut HashMap<String, User>) -> AuthResult {
  1011	    let username = match json_string_field(body, "username") {
  1012	        Some(value) if valid_username(&value) => value,
  1013	        _ => return AuthResult::BadRequest,
  1014	    };
  1015	    let password = match json_string_field(body, "password") {
  1016	        Some(value) if value.len() >= 8 => value,
  1017	        _ => return AuthResult::BadRequest,
  1018	    };
  1019	    let role = match json_string_field(body, "role") {
  1020	        Some(value) if value == "dm" || value == "player" => value,
  1021	        _ => return AuthResult::BadRequest,
  1022	    };
  1023	
  1024	    if users.contains_key(&username) {
  1025	        return AuthResult::Conflict;
  1026	    }
  1027	
  1028	    users.insert(
  1029	        username.clone(),
  1030	        User {
  1031	            username: username.clone(),
  1032	            password_hash: password_hash(&username, &password),
  1033	        },
  1034	    );
  1035	
  1036	    AuthResult::Ok(format!(
  1037	        r#"{{"username":"{}","role":"{}"}}"#,
  1038	        json_escape(&username),
  1039	        json_escape(&role)
  1040	    ))

+fn create_monster(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    let monster = match parse_monster(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CompendiumResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if monster_exists(storage, &monster.slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO compendium_monsters (slug, name, cr, armor_class, hit_points, tags) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&monster.slug),
+        sql_string(&monster.name),
+        sql_string(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points,
+        sql_string(&encode_string_list(&monster.tags))
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CompendiumResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CompendiumResult::Ok(monster_create_json(&monster))
+}
+
+fn read_monster(slug: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    if !valid_slug(slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    match load_monster(storage, slug) {
+        Ok(Some(monster)) => CompendiumResult::Ok(monster_read_json(&monster)),
+        Ok(None) => CompendiumResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => CompendiumResult::StorageError,
+    }
+}
+
+fn create_item(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    let item = match parse_item(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CompendiumResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if item_exists(storage, &item.slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO compendium_items (slug, name, item_type, rarity, cost_gp) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&item.slug),
+        sql_string(&item.name),
+        sql_string(&item.item_type),
+        sql_string(&item.rarity),
+        item.cost_gp
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CompendiumResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CompendiumResult::Ok(item_json(&item))
+}
+
+fn read_item(slug: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    if !valid_slug(slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    match load_item(storage, slug) {
+        Ok(Some(item)) => CompendiumResult::Ok(item_json(&item)),
+        Ok(None) => CompendiumResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => CompendiumResult::StorageError,
+    }
+}
+
+fn parse_monster(body: &str) -> Option<Monster> {
+    let slug = json_string_field(body, "slug")?;
+    if !valid_slug(&slug) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let name = non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?;
+    let cr = non_empty_json_string(body, "cr")?;
+    let armor_class = json_i64_field(body, "armor_class")?;
+    let hit_points = json_i64_field(body, "hit_points")?;
+    let tags = json_string_array_field(body, "tags")?;
+    if armor_class < 0 || hit_points < 0 {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Monster {
+        slug,
+        name,
+        cr,
+        armor_class,
+        hit_points,
+        tags,
+    })
+}
+
+fn parse_item(body: &str) -> Option<Item> {
+    let slug = json_string_field(body, "slug")?;
+    if !valid_slug(&slug) {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let name = non_empty_json_string(body, "name")?;
+    let item_type = non_empty_json_string(body, "type")?;
+    let rarity = non_empty_json_string(body, "rarity")?;
+    let cost_gp = json_i64_field(body, "cost_gp")?;
+    if cost_gp < 0 {
+        return None;
+    }
+    Some(Item {
+        slug,
+        name,
+        item_type,
+        rarity,
+        cost_gp,
+    })
+}
+
+fn non_empty_json_string(body: &str, key: &str) -> Option<String> {
+    match json_string_field(body, key) {
+        Some(value) if !value.is_empty() => Some(value),
+        _ => None,
+    }
+}
+
+fn valid_slug(slug: &str) -> bool {
+    !slug.is_empty()
+        && slug
+            .bytes()
+            .all(|b| b.is_ascii_lowercase() || b.is_ascii_digit() || b == b'-')
+}
+
+fn monster_exists(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug FROM compendium_monsters WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn item_exists(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug FROM compendium_items WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn load_monster(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> Result<Option<Monster>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug, name, cr, armor_class, hit_points, tags FROM compendium_monsters WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(6, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 6 {
+        return Err("malformed monster row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Monster {
+        slug: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        cr: fields[2].to_string(),
+        armor_class: fields[3].parse().map_err(|_| "bad armor_class")?,
+        hit_points: fields[4].parse().map_err(|_| "bad hit_points")?,
+        tags: decode_string_list(fields[5]).ok_or_else(|| "bad tags".to_string())?,
+    }))
+}
+
+fn load_item(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> Result<Option<Item>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug, name, item_type, rarity, cost_gp FROM compendium_items WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(5, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 5 {
+        return Err("malformed item row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Item {
+        slug: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        item_type: fields[2].to_string(),
+        rarity: fields[3].to_string(),
+        cost_gp: fields[4].parse().map_err(|_| "bad cost_gp")?,
+    }))
+}
+
+fn monster_create_json(monster: &Monster) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","cr":"{}","armor_class":{},"hit_points":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&monster.slug),
+        json_escape(&monster.name),
+        json_escape(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points
+    )
+}
+
+fn monster_read_json(monster: &Monster) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","cr":"{}","armor_class":{},"hit_points":{},"tags":[{}]}}"#,
+        json_escape(&monster.slug),
+        json_escape(&monster.name),
+        json_escape(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points,
+        string_array_json(&monster.tags)
+    )
+}
+
+fn item_json(item: &Item) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","type":"{}","rarity":"{}","cost_gp":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&item.slug),
+        json_escape(&item.name),
+        json_escape(&item.item_type),
+        json_escape(&item.rarity),
+        item.cost_gp
+    )
+}
+
+fn string_array_json(values: &[String]) -> String {
+    values
+        .iter()
+        .map(|value| format!(r#""{}""#, json_escape(value)))
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",")
+}
+
+fn encode_string_list(values: &[String]) -> String {
+    values
+        .iter()
+        .map(|value| hex_encode(value))
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",")
+}
+
+fn decode_string_list(encoded: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    if encoded.is_empty() {
+        return Some(Vec::new());
+    }
+    let mut values = Vec::new();
+    for value in encoded.split(',') {
+        values.push(hex_decode(value)?);
+    }
+    Some(values)
+}

+fn json_string_array_field(source: &str, key: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    let body = json_array_field(source, key)?;
+    parse_string_array_body(body)
+}
+
 fn json_object_field<'a>(source: &'a str, key: &str) -> Option<&'a str> {
     let value = field_value(source, key)?;
     balanced_slice(value, '{', '}')
@@ -1121,6 +1464,56 @@
     objects

+fn parse_string_array_body(array_body: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    let mut values = Vec::new();
+    let mut rest = array_body.trim();
+    if rest.is_empty() {
+        return Some(values);
+    }
+    loop {
+        let (value, consumed) = parse_json_string_prefix(rest)?;
+        values.push(value);
+        rest = rest[consumed..].trim_start();
+        if rest.is_empty() {
+            return Some(values);
+        }
+        rest = rest.strip_prefix(',')?.trim_start();
+        if rest.is_empty() {
+            return None;
+        }
+    }
+}
+
+fn parse_json_string_prefix(source: &str) -> Option<(String, usize)> {
+    let bytes = source.as_bytes();
+    if bytes.first().copied()? != b'"' {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let mut out = String::new();
+    let mut escaped = false;
+    for (i, ch) in source[1..].char_indices() {
+        if escaped {
+            match ch {
+                '"' | '\\' | '/' => out.push(ch),
+                'n' => out.push('\n'),
+                'r' => out.push('\r'),
+                't' => out.push('\t'),
+                'b' => out.push('\u{0008}'),
+                'f' => out.push('\u{000c}'),
+                _ => return None,
+            }
+            escaped = false;
+        } else if ch == '\\' {
+            escaped = true;
+        } else if ch == '"' {
+            return Some((out, i + 2));
+        } else {
+            out.push(ch);
+        }
+    }
+    None
+}
+

     if value_twice % 2 == 0 {
         (value_twice / 2).to_string()

+            r#"{"slug":"goblin","name":"Goblin","cr":"1/4","armor_class":15,"hit_points":7,"tags":["humanoid","goblinoid"]}"#
+        );
+    }
+

+        )
+        .unwrap();
+        assert_eq!(
+            item_json(&item),
+            r#"{"slug":"healing-potion","name":"Potion of Healing","type":"potion","rarity":"common","cost_gp":50}"#
+        );
+    }

+        assert_eq!(
+            json_string_array_field(r#"{"tags":[]}"#, "tags"),
+            Some(Vec::new())
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            json_string_array_field(r#"{"tags":["one",]}"#, "tags"),
+            None
+        );

codex
One design choice I’m checking is create status codes. Existing user registration uses `201`, and compendium creates are new records too, so the new endpoints follow that pattern while preserving existing `200` responses elsewhere.

+enum CompendiumResult {
+    Ok(String),
+    BadRequest,
+    NotFound,
+    Conflict,
+    StorageError,
+}
+
+fn create_monster(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    let monster = match parse_monster(body) {
+        Some(value) => value,
+        None => return CompendiumResult::BadRequest,
+    };
+    if monster_exists(storage, &monster.slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::Conflict;
+    }
+    let sql = format!(
+        "INSERT INTO compendium_monsters (slug, name, cr, armor_class, hit_points, tags) VALUES ({}, {}, {}, {}, {}, {});",
+        sql_string(&monster.slug),
+        sql_string(&monster.name),
+        sql_string(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points,
+        sql_string(&encode_string_list(&monster.tags))
+    );
+    if run_sql(storage, &sql).is_err() {
+        return CompendiumResult::StorageError;
+    }
+    CompendiumResult::Ok(monster_create_json(&monster))
+}
+
+fn read_monster(slug: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {
+    if !valid_slug(slug) {
+        return CompendiumResult::BadRequest;
+    }
+    match load_monster(storage, slug) {
+        Ok(Some(monster)) => CompendiumResult::Ok(monster_read_json(&monster)),
+        Ok(None) => CompendiumResult::NotFound,
+        Err(_) => CompendiumResult::StorageError,
+    }
+}
+
+fn create_item(body: &str, storage: &Storage) -> CompendiumResult {

+        None => return CompendiumResult::BadRequest,

+        sql_string(&item.name),
+        sql_string(&item.item_type),

+
+fn item_exists(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> bool {
+    query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug FROM compendium_items WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )
+    .map(|out| !out.trim().is_empty())
+    .unwrap_or(false)
+}
+
+fn load_monster(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> Result<Option<Monster>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug, name, cr, armor_class, hit_points, tags FROM compendium_monsters WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(6, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 6 {
+        return Err("malformed monster row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Monster {
+        slug: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        cr: fields[2].to_string(),
+        armor_class: fields[3].parse().map_err(|_| "bad armor_class")?,
+        hit_points: fields[4].parse().map_err(|_| "bad hit_points")?,
+        tags: decode_string_list(fields[5]).ok_or_else(|| "bad tags".to_string())?,
+    }))
+}
+
+fn load_item(storage: &Storage, slug: &str) -> Result<Option<Item>, String> {
+    let out = query_sql(
+        storage,
+        &format!(
+            "SELECT slug, name, item_type, rarity, cost_gp FROM compendium_items WHERE slug = {} LIMIT 1;",
+            sql_string(slug)
+        ),
+    )?;
+    let Some(line) = out.lines().next() else {
+        return Ok(None);
+    };
+    let fields = line.splitn(5, '\t').collect::<Vec<_>>();
+    if fields.len() != 5 {
+        return Err("malformed item row".to_string());
+    }
+    Ok(Some(Item {
+        slug: fields[0].to_string(),
+        name: fields[1].to_string(),
+        item_type: fields[2].to_string(),
+        rarity: fields[3].to_string(),
+        cost_gp: fields[4].parse().map_err(|_| "bad cost_gp")?,
+    }))
+}
+
+fn monster_create_json(monster: &Monster) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","cr":"{}","armor_class":{},"hit_points":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&monster.slug),
+        json_escape(&monster.name),
+        json_escape(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points
+    )
+}
+
+fn monster_read_json(monster: &Monster) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","cr":"{}","armor_class":{},"hit_points":{},"tags":[{}]}}"#,
+        json_escape(&monster.slug),
+        json_escape(&monster.name),
+        json_escape(&monster.cr),
+        monster.armor_class,
+        monster.hit_points,
+        string_array_json(&monster.tags)
+    )
+}
+
+fn item_json(item: &Item) -> String {
+    format!(
+        r#"{{"slug":"{}","name":"{}","type":"{}","rarity":"{}","cost_gp":{}}}"#,
+        json_escape(&item.slug),
+        json_escape(&item.name),
+        json_escape(&item.item_type),
+        json_escape(&item.rarity),
+        item.cost_gp
+    )
+}
+
+fn string_array_json(values: &[String]) -> String {
+    values
+        .iter()
+        .map(|value| format!(r#""{}""#, json_escape(value)))
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",")
+}
+
+fn encode_string_list(values: &[String]) -> String {
+    values
+        .iter()
+        .map(|value| hex_encode(value))
+        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
+        .join(",")
+}
+
+fn decode_string_list(encoded: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    if encoded.is_empty() {
+        return Some(Vec::new());
+    }
+    let mut values = Vec::new();
+    for value in encoded.split(',') {
+        values.push(hex_decode(value)?);
+    }
+    Some(values)
+}
+

         Some(value) if valid_username(&value) => value,

 }
 
+fn json_string_array_field(source: &str, key: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    let body = json_array_field(source, key)?;
+    parse_string_array_body(body)
+}
+
 fn json_object_field<'a>(source: &'a str, key: &str) -> Option<&'a str> {
     let value = field_value(source, key)?;
     balanced_slice(value, '{', '}')
@@ -1121,6 +1464,56 @@
     objects
 }
 
+fn parse_string_array_body(array_body: &str) -> Option<Vec<String>> {
+    let mut values = Vec::new();
+    let mut rest = array_body.trim();
+    if rest.is_empty() {
+        return Some(values);
+    }
+    loop {
+        let (value, consumed) = parse_json_string_prefix(rest)?;
+        values.push(value);
+        rest = rest[consumed..].trim_start();
+        if rest.is_empty() {
+            return Some(values);
+        }
+        rest = rest.strip_prefix(',')?.trim_start();
+        if rest.is_empty() {
+            return None;
+        }
+    }
+}
+
+fn parse_json_string_prefix(source: &str) -> Option<(String, usize)> {
+    let bytes = source.as_bytes();
+    if bytes.first().copied()? != b'"' {
+        return None;
+    }
+    let mut out = String::new();
+    let mut escaped = false;
+    for (i, ch) in source[1..].char_indices() {
+        if escaped {
+            match ch {
+                '"' | '\\' | '/' => out.push(ch),
+                'n' => out.push('\n'),
+                'r' => out.push('\r'),
+                't' => out.push('\t'),
+                'b' => out.push('\u{0008}'),
+                'f' => out.push('\u{000c}'),
+                _ => return None,
+            }
+            escaped = false;
+        } else if ch == '\\' {
+            escaped = true;
+        } else if ch == '"' {
+            return Some((out, i + 2));
+        } else {
+            out.push(ch);
+        }
+    }
+    None
+}
+
 fn number_from_halves(value_twice: i64) -> String {
     if value_twice % 2 == 0 {
         (value_twice / 2).to_string()
@@ -1335,4 +1728,44 @@
             )
         );
     }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn monster_json_matches_create_and_read_contract() {
+        let monster = parse_monster(
+            r#"{"slug":"goblin","name":"Goblin","cr":"1/4","armor_class":15,"hit_points":7,"tags":["humanoid","goblinoid"]}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+        assert_eq!(
+            monster_create_json(&monster),
+            r#"{"slug":"goblin","name":"Goblin","cr":"1/4","armor_class":15,"hit_points":7}"#
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            monster_read_json(&monster),
+            r#"{"slug":"goblin","name":"Goblin","cr":"1/4","armor_class":15,"hit_points":7,"tags":["humanoid","goblinoid"]}"#
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn item_json_matches_contract() {
+        let item = parse_item(
+            r#"{"slug":"healing-potion","name":"Potion of Healing","type":"potion","rarity":"common","cost_gp":50}"#,
+        )
+        .unwrap();
+        assert_eq!(
+            item_json(&item),
+            r#"{"slug":"healing-potion","name":"Potion of Healing","type":"potion","rarity":"common","cost_gp":50}"#
+        );
+    }
+
+    #[test]
+    fn string_array_parser_accepts_empty_and_rejects_trailing_comma() {
+        assert_eq!(
+            json_string_array_field(r#"{"tags":[]}"#, "tags"),
+            Some(Vec::new())
+        );
+        assert_eq!(
+            json_string_array_field(r#"{"tags":["one",]}"#, "tags"),
+            None
+        );
+    }

   293	
   294	fn respond(stream: &mut TcpStream, status: u16, body: &str) -> std::io::Result<()> {
   295	    let label = match status {
   296	        200 => "OK",
   297	        201 => "Created",
   298	        400 => "Bad Request",
   299	        401 => "Unauthorized",
   300	        404 => "Not Found",
   301	        409 => "Conflict",
   302	        500 => "Internal Server Error",
   303	        _ => "Error",
   304	    };
   305	    write!(
   306	        stream,
   307	        "HTTP/1.1 {status} {label}\r\nContent-Type: application/json\r\nContent-Length: {}\r\nConnection: close\r\n\r\n{}",
   308	        body.len(),
   309	        body
   310	    )
   311	}
   312	
   313	fn init_storage(storage: &Storage) -> Result<(), String> {
   314	    run_sql(
   315	        storage,
   316	        &format!(
   317	            "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS meta (key TEXT PRIMARY KEY, value TEXT NOT NULL);
   318	             CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (username TEXT PRIMARY KEY, password_hash TEXT NOT NULL);
   319	             CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS combat_sessions (id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, data TEXT NOT NULL);
   320	             CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS compendium_monsters (slug TEXT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT NOT NULL, cr TEXT NOT NULL, armor_class INTEGER NOT NULL, hit_points INTEGER NOT NULL, tags TEXT NOT NULL);
   321	             CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS compendium_items (slug TEXT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT NOT NULL, item_type TEXT NOT NULL, rarity TEXT NOT NULL, cost_gp INTEGER NOT NULL);
   322	             INSERT OR REPLACE INTO meta (key, value) VALUES ('schema_version', '{}');",
   323	            SCHEMA_VERSION
   324	        ),
   325	    )
   326	}
   327	
   328	fn reset_storage(storage: &Storage) -> Result<(), String> {
   329	    let _ = std::fs::remove_file(&storage.db_path);
   330	    init_storage(storage)
